English

Since verbs meaning ’to go’ or ’to move’ mean also ’to have a knowledge of’ or ‘to know’,
the root pad in the word prapadye, which means ’to go’
means, here the specific knowledge required in this context.

Espa├▒ol

la ra├нz “pad” de la palabra prapadye, que significa ‘ir’
significa, aqu├н el conocimiento espec├нfico requerido en este contexto.

English

This excellence or intensity of faith would arise
only when one bears in mind
the mediatorship (of Lakс╣гm─л) and one’s relationship with the Lord,
the Lord’s qualities and the like (form)
which are respectively present in the words (┼Ъr─лmat) and N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa.

las cualidades del Se├▒or y similares (forma)
que est├бn respectivamente presentes en las palabras (┼Ъr─лmat) y N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa.

Is not His grace of such a nature
as is described in the ┼Ыloka,
about such things as even anjali :-

y conducir a la consecuci├│n de cosas buenas.

(in those who have performed prapatti with all its aс╣Еgas).

(en aquellos que han realizado prapatti con todos sus aс╣Еgas).

рдЙрдкрд╛рдпрдореН рдЖрдЧрд╡реН рдЕрдзреНрдпрд╡рд╕рд┐рдХреНрдХрд┐рд▒реЗрдйреН

рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рдорд╣рд╛рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕рддреНрддреИрдЪреН рдЪреКрд▓реНрд▓

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЗрддреНрдердореН “рдЙрдкрд╛рдпрддреНрд╡реЗрди рдЕрдзреНрдпрд╡рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдореА"рддрд┐ рдорд╣рд╛-рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕рдпреН рдЙрдХреНрддреЗ рд╕рддрд┐,

English

On this expression of intense faith stating,

“I have made up my mind
to beg Thee for being my up─Бya”,

Espa├▒ol

Ante esta expresi├│n de intensa fe que afirma,

“Ya he tomado una decisi├│n
para rogar que seas mi up─Бya”,

рдЗрд╖реНрдЯ-рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддреНрдпреН–рдЕ-рдирд┐рд╖реНрдЯ-рдирд┐рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐–рд░реВрдк -рдлрд▓-рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердирд╛рдпрд╛рдореН

рдкреБрдирд░реБрдХреНрддрд┐рдГ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН ред

English

It may be asked:–

" What is the prayer in this first part of Dvaya for?
Since in the second part,
there is a prayer for the attainment of the desired end
and the removal of hindrances thereto,
the prayer here cannot be for the same
as, in that case, there would be repetition or redundancy.

Espa├▒ol

Se puede preguntar:–

“┬┐Para qu├й sirve la oraci├│n de esta primera parte del Dvaya?
Ya que en la segunda parte,
hay una oraci├│n para la consecuci├│n del fin deseado
y la eliminaci├│n de obst├бculos al mismo,
la oraci├│n aqu├н no puede ser por lo mismo
ya que, en ese caso, habr├нa repetici├│n o redundancia.

English

The sum and substance of the first and the second parts, when duly determined,
will amount to saying this :-

“I am destitute of all up─Бyas;
therefore in order that Thou mayst stand in the place of these up├гyas
and grant me the specific end that is desired,
I surrender the responsibility for the protection of myself as stated ( in the ┼Ы─Бstras)”.

Thus it (the Dvaya) is a surrender of the responsibility (for protection)
accompanied by a special prayer.

Espa├▒ol

La suma y sustancia de la primera y la segunda parte, cuando est├йn debidamente determinadas,
equivaldr├б a decir esto:-

“Yo estoy desprovisto de todos los up─Бyas;
por lo tanto, para que T├║ puedas estar en el lugar de estos up├гyas
y conc├йdeme el fin espec├нfico que se desea,

Yo entrego la responsabilidad de la protecci├│n de m├н mismo como declarado (en los ┼Ы─Бstras)”.

Por lo tanto (el Dvaya) es una rendici├│n de la responsabilidad (de protecci├│n)
acompa├▒ado de una oraci├│n especial.

who has the gift of mokс╣гa in His power,

which can be accomplished by the aspirant to mukti
in accordance with the ┼Ы─Бstras.

English

Since prapatti ordains, as an up─Бya, the surrender of the responsibility for protection (bharasamarpana)
which is adapted to the adhik─Бr─л
who is destitute of up─Бyas,
it goes without saying (from the very logic of the matter) that
it does not require the performance of any other action
which is too hard (for him) to perform.

Espa├▒ol

Puesto que prapatti ordena, como up─Бya, la entrega de la responsabilidad de protecci├│n (bharasamarpana)

que est├б adaptado al adhik─Бr─л
quien est├б desprovisto de up─Бyas,

no hace falta decir (desde la l├│gica misma del asunto) que
no requiere la realizaci├│n de ninguna otra acci├│n
lo cual es demasiado dif├нcil (para ├йl) de realizar.

Thus in the word prapadye (I resolve to seek) accompanied by the word saranam (refuge),
four accessories may be considered as having been indicated:

the faith that (the Lord) will protect,
and so also seeking Him as the Saviour,
the surrender of the self
and (one’s) helplessness (k─Бrpaс╣Зya).

la fe que (el Se├▒or) proteger├б,
y as├н tambi├йn busc├бndolo como Salvador,
la rendici├│n del yo

that these accessories, too, are to be thought of only once

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрд╛-рдкрджреЗ рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рди-рд╡реНрдпрдкрджреЗрд╢реЛ
рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд░реН-рд▓рд╡рдирд╛рджрд┐-рдордиреНрддреНрд░реЗрд╖реНрд╡реН рдЗрд╡рд╛рдиреБрд╖реНрдард╛рди-рдХрд╛рд▓рд╛рднрд┐рдкреНрд░рд╛рдпрдГ ред

English

The use of the present tense in the verb (prapadye) is,
like (the use of present tense in the verb occurring in) the mantra uttered while cutting ku┼Ыa grass,
to indicate the time when the prapatti is performed.
(It does not mean, as the present tense sometimes means,
that it should be done always).

Espa├▒ol

El uso del tiempo presente en el verbo (prapadye) es,
como (el uso del tiempo presente en el verbo que ocurre en) el mantra pronunciado mientras corta hierba ku┼Ыa,
para indicar el momento en que se realiza el prapatti.
(No significa, como a veces significa el tiempo presente,
que se debe hacer siempre).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрдиреИрд╡рдореНрднрд╛рд╡реЗрди -

‘рдЕрдпрдВ рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рди-рд╡реНрдпрдкрджреЗрд╢реЛ рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рди-рджреЗрд╣рд╛рд╡рдзрд┐рдХрддрдпрд╛ рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддреНрдпрдиреБрд╖реНрдард╛рди-рдХрд░реНрддрд╡реНрдпрддрд╛рдВ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рддреАрддрд┐’,

English

The views ( held by some )

That the present tense (in prapadye) shows that
the intention is to enjoin the continuous performance of prapatti until the end of the present body,

Espa├▒ol

Las opiniones (sostenidas por algunos)

Que el tiempo presente (en prapadye) muestra que
la intenci├│n es para ordenar la realizaci├│n continua de prapatti
hasta el final del presente cuerpo,

English

Therefore the use of the present tense in this sentence (in Dvaya)
which states the up─Бya
does not refer to the continuance of uttering the Dvaya
for the sake of the enjoyment arising from love
which is expressed in ┼Ъr─л R─Бm─Бnuja’s Gadya (namely - uttering the Dvaya always with an understanding of its meaning).

(The meaning is:
as an up─Бya a single performance or utterance will do;
but when one finds it enjoyable,
the Dvaya may be repeatedly uttered).

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, el uso del tiempo presente en esta oraci├│n (en Dvaya)
que enuncia el up─Бya
no se refiere a la continuaci├│n de pronunciar el Dvaya
por el disfrute que surge del amor
que se expresa en el Gadya de ┼Ъr─л R─Бm─Бnuja (es decir, - pronunciar el Dvaya siempre con una comprensi├│n de su significado).

(El significado es:
como up─Бya, una sola actuaci├│n o enunciaci├│n servir├б;
pero cuando uno lo encuentra divertido,
el Dvaya puede ser repetidamente pronunciado).
